[21/11/21, 3:55:54‚ÄØPM] CM Jagdish-CREA(I) VP: *IMPORTANT NOTE & GUIDELINES  - YOUR CREA (I) WHATSAPP / TELEGRAM GROUP POSTINGS* 


For the benefit of our members in particular and the Association in general, we are once again highlighting the guidelines to be strictly followed while posting messages in *Your CREA (I) WhatsApp / Telegram Group.*

1) *TIMINGS FOR POSTINGS*
Strictly between 8.00 AM to 9.00 PM. 

2) *WHAT TO POST*
Only messages related to Real Estate availability and requirements.

 *NO GOOD MORNING/ GOOD NIGHT POSTS AT ALL. NO POSITIVE THOUGHTS / FUN / MOCKERY POSTS/ MESSAGES.* 
 
3) *PHOTOS*
Maximum of 2 photos related to Real Estate inventory. 

4) *VIDEOS*
Please post link to the videos & not the video itself

No photos / videos of Developer Projects as a backdrop or in the interest of promoting their projects as a whole.

*5) CONGRATULATORY MESSAGES*
Please send Congratulatory messages to other members only on their private windows. Let‚Äôs keep this group confined to inventory & requirements only. 

Members are requested to strictly follow the above guidelines and *VIOLATION* of any guideline will invite delisting. 
*First Violation* - 3 days
*Second Violation* - 1 week 
*Third Violation* - Admin to take suitable action

Please follow these Guidelines to help yourself and others to conduct business. 

*We value your membership and commitment to CREA (I). Privileged to have you as a fellow member and colleague.* 

*Warmest Regards*,

*Manager- CREA (I)*                  
*On behalf of the Managing Committee.*

Bhagwan ke ghar der hai, andher nahi üôè

Given the circumstances and developing COVID situation, the Govt. Of Karnataka has imposed restrictions on maximum number of people for an Event till Jan 22 extendable to Mar 22 or later. Keeping in mind the safety norms and CREA (I) 's unanimous decision in conjunction with NAR India Leadership Team and Core Committee, the difficult but correct decision has been reached to postpone the 14th NAR India Convention to be held in Bangalore from March 2022 to *6th and 7th August 2022*

The vigour, the enthusiasm, the venue & the commitment remains the same. Only the dates have changed.

All Registrations done will hold good. Please also note the GB and the AGM will be held in Bangalore in March, as scheduled earlier.

Waqt badla hai, Ham nahi üôèüôè Thank you all for your cooperation and understanding and for the support you will render to CREA (I) in this difficult decision. We look forward to welcome you all on 6th and 7th August in better weather of Bangalore üôè
